				<h1><a href="showtutorial.php?tutorialid=22">How to Send SMS using Java Program (full code sample included)</a></h1>
				
				<p>By: Emiley J.<!-- Viewed: 62519 times --> Emailed: 1145 times  Printed: 144 times &nbsp; <g:plusone></g:plusone> &nbsp; <iframe src="//www.facebook.com/plugins/like.php?href=http%3A%2F%2Fwww.facebook.com%2Fjavasamples&amp;send=false&amp;layout=button_count&amp;width=100&amp;show_faces=false&amp;action=like&amp;colorscheme=light&amp;font&amp;height=21&amp;appId=130385813687284" scrolling="no" frameborder="0" style="border:none; overflow:hidden; width:90px; height:21px;" allowTransparency="true"></iframe></p>

<div style="color:#000080;font-family:Arial;font-size:10pt">
<p>You can use this free Java sample program to send SMS from your PC using GSM
modem connected to your computer to your COM port. You also need to download and
install the <a href="http://java.sun.com/products/javacomm/">Java comm api from
Sun</a>.</p>
<p>This program needs the following java files to function.
<p>1. SerialConnection.java (This file is used to connect to your COM port from
    your java program)<br><br>
2. SerialConnectionException.java (This file is for handling serial
    connection exceptions in your Java program)<br><br>
3. SerialParameters.java (This program is used to set your COM port
    properties for connecting to your com port from your java program)<br><br>
4. Sender.java (This is the program that implements runnable and sends SMS
    using the serial connection)<br><br>
5. SMSClient.java (This java class is the main class that can be instantiated
    in your own java program and called to send SMS. This program in turn will
    use all the above four files internally to send out your SMS).<br>
</p>
<p><a href="http://www.java-samples.com/java/sms.rar">Download Send SMS Java
sample program files</a></p>
<pre>/*
 *
 * A free Java sample program 
 * A list of java programs to send SMS using your COM serial connection
 * and a GSM modem
 *
 * @author William Alexander
 * free for use as long as this comment is included 
 * in the program as it is
 * 
 * More Free Java programs available for download 
 * at http://www.java-samples.com
 *
 *
 * Note: to use this program you need to download all the 5 java files
 * mentioned on top
 *
 */
public class SMSClient implements Runnable{

  public final static int SYNCHRONOUS=0;
  public final static int ASYNCHRONOUS=1;
  private Thread myThread=null;

  private int mode=-1;
  private String recipient=null;
  private String message=null;

  public int status=-1;
  public long messageNo=-1;


  public SMSClient(int mode) {
      this.mode=mode;
    }

  public int sendMessage (String recipient, String message){
    this.recipient=recipient;
    this.message=message;
    //System.out.println(&quot;recipient: &quot; + recipient + &quot; message: &quot; + message);
    myThread = new Thread(this);
    myThread.start();
//    run();
    return status;
    }
    public void run(){

    Sender aSender = new Sender(recipient,message);

    try{
      //send message
          aSender.send ();

         // System.out.println(&quot;sending ... &quot;);

      //in SYNCHRONOUS mode wait for return : 0 for OK,
      //-2 for timeout, -1 for other errors
      if (mode==SYNCHRONOUS) {
          while (aSender.status == -1){
            myThread.sleep (1000);
          }
      }
      if (aSender.status == 0) messageNo=aSender.messageNo ;

    }catch (Exception e){

        e.printStackTrace();

    }

    this.status=aSender.status ;

    aSender=null;


  }
}</pre>

the deployment of the .so &amp; java.comm jar is done as per requirement<br />

our application is based on the following code: <br />

<br />
we have complied java files...then we have written the shell file for running the java class file.<br />
<br />
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------<br />
//DemoSms.java<br />
public class DemoSms<br />
{<br />
	public static void main(String args[])<br />
	{<br />
		SMSClient sc = new SMSClient(1);<br />
		sc.sendMessage(&quot;MyCellNo&quot;,&quot;Hello&quot;);<br />
	}<br />
<br />
}<br />
//ends here<br />
<br />
<br />
#shell file<br />
<br />
JAVA_HOME=/opt/jdk1.5.0_12<br />
CLASSPATH=/opt/sms:$JAVA_HOME/jre/lib/comm.jar<br />
<br />
$JAVA_HOME/bin/java -cp $CLASSPATH DemoSms<br />
<br />
#shell file ends here<br />
<br />
<br />
<br />
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------<br />
/*<br />

*/<br />

I can send sms successfully from Windows XP, by using the java codes.<br />
I found very very simple codes.<br />
<br />
Please check this one and inform me if you cannot deploy.<br />
<br />
But please be sure all things first. I am trying trying to send in Linux , open SUSE... <br />
<br />
1. Please try to send SMS via Hyper Terminal first. Don't try my code before you can send message form hyper terminal first.<br />
<br />
(My modem is quite old Wavecom. WMOD2, for that one you can use standard driver, I use the 9600 bps.)<br />
<br />
Try to make sure the COM port and the modem setting you chose in HyperTerminal to be matched. Otherwise when you type &quot;AT&quot;, it will show funny characters in hyper terminal.<br />
<br />
And I am now doing for my customer's SMS authentication program.<br />
<br />
import javax.comm.*;<br />
import java.io.*;<br />
import java.util.*;<br />
import java.lang.*;<br />
<br />
public class SerialWrite implements Runnable, SerialPortEventListener<br />
{<br />
static String output=&quot;&quot;;<br />
public void run()<br />
{}<br />
<br />
static Enumeration portList;<br />
static CommPortIdentifier portId;<br />
static String dest = &quot;+6596123116&quot;;<br />
static String messageString = &quot;Hello Testing11&quot;;<br />
InputStream inputStream;<br />
<br />
static SerialPort serialPort;<br />
static OutputStream outputStream;<br />
<br />
public void serialEvent(SerialPortEvent event)<br />
{<br />
switch (event.getEventType())<br />
{<br />
case SerialPortEvent.BI:<br />
case SerialPortEvent.OE:<br />
case SerialPortEvent.FE:<br />
case SerialPortEvent.PE:<br />
case SerialPortEvent.CD:<br />
case SerialPortEvent.CTS:<br />
case SerialPortEvent.DSR:<br />
case SerialPortEvent.RI:<br />
case SerialPortEvent.OUTPUT_BUFFER_EMPTY:<br />
System.out.println(&quot;Error&quot;);<br />
break;<br />
case SerialPortEvent.DATA_AVAILABLE:<br />
{<br />
<br />
BufferedReader reader = new BufferedReader(new InputStreamReader(inputStream));<br />
String line = &quot;&quot;;<br />
try<br />
{<br />
<br />
while ( (line = reader.readLine()) != null)<br />
{<br />
<br />
if(line.equalsIgnoreCase(&quot;OK&quot;) || (line.indexOf(&quot;+CMGS&quot;) != -1))<br />
{<br />
output=line;<br />
<br />
}<br />
Thread.sleep(10);<br />
<br />
}<br />
}<br />
catch (Exception e)<br />
{<br />
System.err.println(&quot;Error while reading Port &quot; + e);<br />
}<br />
break;<br />
<br />
}<br />
} //switch<br />
}<br />
<br />
public SerialWrite(SerialPort serial)<br />
{<br />
try<br />
{<br />
inputStream = serial.getInputStream();<br />
try<br />
{<br />
serial.addEventListener(this);<br />
}<br />
catch (TooManyListenersException e)<br />
{<br />
System.out.println(&quot;Exception in Adding Listener&quot; + e);<br />
}<br />
serial.notifyOnDataAvailable(true);<br />
<br />
}<br />
catch (Exception ex)<br />
{<br />
System.out.println(&quot;Exception in getting InputStream&quot; + ex);<br />
}<br />
<br />
}<br />
<br />
public static void main(String[] args) throws Exception<br />
{<br />
int i=0;<br />
//String line0 = &quot;ATZ\r\n&quot;;<br />
String line1 = &quot;AT+CMGF=1\r\n&quot;;<br />
//String line2 = &quot;AT+CSCA=\&quot;+6581867612\&quot;\r\n&quot;;<br />
<br />
//String line3 = &quot;AT+CMGS=&quot;&quot;\&quot;&quot; dest + &quot;\&quot;&quot;+&quot;\r\n&quot;;<br />
//String line3 = &quot;AT+CMGw=&quot;+&quot;\&quot;&quot;+ args[0] + &quot;\&quot;&quot;+&quot;\r\n&quot;;<br />
String line3 = &quot;AT+CMGS=&quot;+&quot;\&quot;&quot;+ args[0] + &quot;\&quot;&quot;+&quot;\r\n&quot;;<br />
System.out.println(&quot;This &quot;+ line3);<br />
//String line4 = messageString;<br />
String line4 = args[1];<br />
<br />
portList = CommPortIdentifier.getPortIdentifiers();<br />
while (portList.hasMoreElements())<br />
{<br />
portId = (CommPortIdentifier) portList.nextElement();<br />
if (portId.getPortType() == CommPortIdentifier.PORT_SERIAL)<br />
{<br />
System.out.println(&quot;SMS Sending........&quot;);<br />
if ( portId.getName().equals(&quot;COM1&quot;))<br />
{<br />
<br />
System.out.println(&quot;SMS Sending....Port Found&quot;);<br />
try<br />
{<br />
serialPort = (SerialPort) portId.open(&quot;SerialTestApp&quot;, 2000);<br />
SerialWrite wr = new SerialWrite(serialPort);<br />
}<br />
catch (PortInUseException e)<br />
{<br />
System.out.println(&quot;Port In Use &quot; + e);<br />
}<br />
try<br />
{<br />
outputStream = serialPort.getOutputStream();<br />
}<br />
catch (IOException e)<br />
{<br />
System.out.println(&quot;Error writing to output stream &quot; + e);<br />
}<br />
try<br />
{<br />
serialPort.setSerialPortParams(<br />
9600,<br />
SerialPort.DATABITS_8,<br />
SerialPort.STOPBITS_1,<br />
SerialPort.PARITY_NONE);<br />
}<br />
catch (UnsupportedCommOperationException e)<br />
{<br />
System.out.println(&quot;Error&quot;);<br />
}<br />
try<br />
{<br />
<br />
//outputStream.write(line0.getBytes());<br />
//Thread.sleep(10);<br />
//while(!output.equalsIgnoreCase(&quot;ok&quot;))<br />
<br />
//Thread.sleep(10);<br />
//<br />
System.out.println(&quot;It seems OK now&quot;);<br />
<br />
output=&quot;&quot;;<br />
outputStream.write(line1.getBytes());<br />
while(!output.equalsIgnoreCase(&quot;ok&quot;))<br />
Thread.sleep(10);<br />
<br />
<br />
output=&quot;&quot;;<br />
<br />
//outputStream.write(line2.getBytes());<br />
//while(!output.equalsIgnoreCase(&quot;ok&quot;))<br />
//Thread.sleep(10);<br />
<br />
output=&quot;&quot;;<br />
<br />
outputStream.write(line3.getBytes());<br />
Thread.sleep(10);<br />
System.out.println(&quot;It seems OK now3&quot;);<br />

System.out.println(&quot;This one is output&quot;+output);<br />
for(i=0;i&lt;3;i++)<br />
{<br />
<br />
outputStream.write(line4.getBytes());<br />

outputStream.write(26);<br />

outputStream.flush();<br />
System.out.println(&quot;This one is outputaaaaa  &quot;+output);<br />
while(!output.equalsIgnoreCase(&quot;ok&quot;))<br />
Thread.sleep(10);<br />
System.out.println(&quot;This one is outputdfsdfsdf:&quot;+output);<br />

}<br />

}<br />
catch (IOException e)<br />

You are probably using threads to send sms. Maybe the one of the thread is still using the port while another thread tries to send out. You could probably use a queue. Save the messages you want to send out in a database first. Then write a program that picks up one by one from this database and sends out. Once sent out, set a flag so that it wont be sent again.<br />
<br />
Do not give up. Many people have used and implemented this code successfully, it only needs a bit of a tweak here and there based on your own setup.</code><br><br> <a href='http://www.java-samples.com/showtutorial.php?tutorialid=22'>View Tutorial</a> &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;By: <a rel="nofollow" href="http://www.java-samples.com">Ramlak</a> at 2009-01-29 20:03:14</TD></TR><TR><TD valign="top" >182. </td><td><a href="showcomment.php?commentid=33789">View Comment</a><br><br><code>Hi Ramlak,<br />

<br />
to all people who are having the problem of <br />
javax.comm.NoSuchPortException<br />
first check if ur COM port is really been detected by the driver ( as it was not in my case) ...thats the reason u'll get this problem!!! .. i'll give you one program that will display all the serial and parallel ports in ur system .. just check if ur port is there or not....<br />
<br />
/* program*/<br />
<br />
import javax.comm.*;<br />
import java.util.Enumeration;<br />
<br />
public class ListPorts {<br />
  public static void main(String args[]) {<br />
    Enumeration ports = CommPortIdentifier.getPortIdentifiers();<br />
    while (ports.hasMoreElements()) {<br />
      CommPortIdentifier port = (CommPortIdentifier)ports.nextElement();<br />
      String type;<br />
      switch (port.getPortType()) {<br />
        case CommPortIdentifier.PORT_PARALLEL:<br />
          type = &quot;Parallel&quot;; <br />
          break;<br />
        case CommPortIdentifier.PORT_SERIAL:<br />
          type = &quot;Serial&quot;; <br />
          break;<br />
        default:  /// Shouldn't happen<br />
          type = &quot;Unknown&quot;; <br />
          break;<br />
      }<br />
      System.out.println(port.getName() + &quot;: &quot; + type);<br />
    }<br />
  }<br />
}<br />
<br />
just check it ...<br />
this is what the output will be!!( my case)<br />
<br />
COM1: Serial<br />
COM2: Serial<br />
COM7: Serial<br />
LPT1: Parallel<br />
LPT2: Parallel<br />
 my port is COM7 .. so just check it !!!!<br />
<br />
Regards ..... Ashish!!!</code><br><br> <a href='http://www.java-samples.com/showtutorial.php?tutorialid=22'>View Tutorial</a> &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;By: <a rel="nofollow" href="">Ashish</a> at 2009-03-25 04:28:25</TD></TR><TR><TD valign="top" >202. </td><td><a href="showcomment.php?commentid=33895">View Comment</a><br><br><code>Please let me know the SMSConnector number of any service provider, kindly mention the service provider name. You don't <br />

the first step. You also must copy the shared library to the bin <br />
directory, and the javax.comm.properties file to the lib directory <br />
of the runtime environment.<br />
<br />
or simply....<br />
copy comm.jar \jdk1.3\jre\lib\ext<br />
copy win32com.dll \jdk1.3\bin<br />
copy javax.comm.properties \jdk1.3\jre\lib<br />
<br />
and also put the win32com.dll to system32 folder..<br />

Sandeep <br />
try this code to find your system ports, and use available ports on sender.java<br />
<br />
import javax.comm.*;<br />
import java.util.Enumeration;<br />
<br />
public class ListPorts {<br />
  public static void main(String args[]) {<br />
    Enumeration ports = CommPortIdentifier.getPortIdentifiers();	<br />
    while (ports.hasMoreElements()) {	<br />
      CommPortIdentifier port = (CommPortIdentifier)ports.nextElement();<br />
      String type;	<br />
      switch (port.getPortType()) {<br />
        case CommPortIdentifier.PORT_PARALLEL:<br />
          type = &quot;Parallel&quot;; <br />
          break;<br />
        case CommPortIdentifier.PORT_SERIAL:<br />
          type = &quot;Serial&quot;; <br />
          break;<br />
        default:  /// Shouldn't happen<br />
          type = &quot;Unknown&quot;; <br />
          break;<br />
      }<br />
      System.out.println(port.getName() + &quot;: &quot; + type);<br />
    }<br />
  }<br />
}<br />
<br />
UU,<br />
<br />
 i suggest you to try the at commands at sender.java on hyperterminal. <br />
<br />
may be issue with the SMSC number.<br />

<br />
1 Add main() method in code.<br />
<br />
 public static void main(String args[]) {<br />
     SMSClient a = new SMSClient(1); //<br />
// arg 1 - send number<br />
// arg 2 - Message<br />
     a.sendMessage(&quot;+91111100&quot;, &quot;11111&quot;);<br />
    }<br />
<br />
2 - Download [from net]  javax.Comm jar (javax.comm.NoSuchPortException )    <br />
    comm.jar <br />
    win32com.dll <br />
    javax.comm.properties<br />
    Make sure all 3 file should be in same folder<br />
<br />
3 - Configure Message center<br />
    Message Center number is available on mobile, check following options<br />
    Goto Messaging &gt; Options &gt; Settings &gt; Text message &gt; Service centre<br />
    Update the number on class.Sender.csca [variable]</code><br><br> <a href='http://www.java-samples.com/showtutorial.php?tutorialid=22'>View Tutorial</a> &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;By: <a rel="nofollow" href="http://www.java-samples.com">Ajay</a> at 2010-09-04 03:01:24</TD></TR><TR><TD valign="top" >376. </td><td><a href="showcomment.php?commentid=35307">View Comment</a><br><br><code>hello everyone<br />

<br />
Use this code to check if that COM port is available..<br />
<br />
private static boolean isPortAvailable(int port) {  <br />
   <br />
try {  <br />
   <br />
ServerSocket srv = new ServerSocket(port);  <br />
  <br />
srv.close();  <br />
srv = null;  <br />
return true;  <br />
   <br />
} catch (IOException e) {  <br />
return false;  <br />
}  <br />
}</code><br><br> <a href='http://www.java-samples.com/showtutorial.php?tutorialid=22'>View Tutorial</a> &nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;By: <a rel="nofollow" href="http://www.java-samples.com">Ramlak</a> at 2011-01-14 21:59:39</TD></TR><TR><TD valign="top" >417. </td><td><a href="showcomment.php?commentid=35778">View Comment</a><br><br><code>Hi.. package practice_servlet;<br />
<br />
import java.io.IOException;<br />
import javax.servlet.ServletException;<br />
import javax.servlet.http.HttpServlet;<br />
import javax.servlet.http.HttpServletRequest;<br />
import javax.servlet.http.HttpServletResponse;<br />
<br />
import practice_bean.practice_bean;<br />
import practice_bo.practice_bo;<br />
<br />
/**<br />
 * Servlet implementation class practice_servlet<br />
 */<br />
public class practice_servlet extends HttpServlet {<br />
	private static final long serialVersionUID = 1L;<br />
	private practice_servlet set;<br />
       <br />
    /**<br />
     * @see HttpServlet#HttpServlet()<br />
     */<br />
    public practice_servlet() {<br />
        super();<br />
        // TODO Auto-generated constructor stub<br />
    }<br />
<br />
	/**<br />
	 * @see HttpServlet#doGet(HttpServletRequest request, HttpServletResponse response)<br />
	 */<br />
	protected void doGet(HttpServletRequest request, HttpServletResponse response) throws ServletException, IOException {<br />
		// TODO Auto-generated method stub<br />
	}<br />
<br />
	/**<br />
	 * @see HttpServlet#doPost(HttpServletRequest request, HttpServletResponse response)<br />
	 */<br />
	protected void doPost(HttpServletRequest request, HttpServletResponse response) throws ServletException, IOException {<br />
		// TODO Auto-generated method stub<br />
		practice_bean practice_beanobj = new practice_bean();<br />
		practice_bo practice_boobj = new practice_bo();<br />
		String username = request.getParameter(&quot;txt_username&quot;);<br />
        String password = request.getParameter(&quot;txt_password&quot;);<br />
       <br />
        practice_beanobj.setUsername(username);<br />
        practice_beanobj.setPassword(password);<br />
  <br />
        practice_boobj.asign(practice_beanobj);<br />
  <br />
	} <br />
   	<br />
<br />
}<br />

        {<br />
    <br />

            return true;<br />
            else <br />

                alert (&quot;enter valid username&quot;);<br />
                return false;<br />
            }<br />

import java.util.Date;<br />
<br />
<br />
public class Sender implements Runnable  {<br />
<br />
 <br />
SerialConnection mySerial =null;<br />
<br />
  <br />
static final private char cntrlZ=(char)26;<br />
  <br />
String in, out;<br />
 <br />
Thread aThread=null;<br />
  <br />
String recipient=null;<br />
  <br />
String message=null;<br />
<br />
  <br />
private String csca=&quot;+919840011003&quot;; // the message center<br />
  <br />
private SerialParameters defaultParameters= new SerialParameters (&quot;COM14&quot;,460800,0,0,8,1,0);<br />
  <br />
public Sender(String recipient, String message){<br />
<br />
    <br />
this.recipient=recipient;<br />
    <br />
this.message=message;<br />
<br />
  <br />
}<br />
  <br />
/**<br />
   * connect to the port and start the dialogue thread<br />
   */<br />
  <br />
public int send () throws Exception{<br />
<br />
    <br />
SerialParameters params = defaultParameters;<br />
<br />
    <br />
mySerial =new SerialConnection (params);<br />
<br />
    <br />
mySerial.openConnection();<br />
<br />
    <br />
aThread=new Thread(this);<br />
<br />
    <br />
aThread.start() ;<br />
    <br />
return 0;<br />
 <br />
 }<br />
<br />
 <br />
 /**<br />
   * implement the dialogue thread,<br />

I have taken some steps for resolving some earlier problems.<br />
Step 1: By the help Of Stackoverflow.com (http://stackoverflow.com/questions/11983764/getting-a-javax-comm-nosuchportexception-when-the-port-exist)<br />
<br />
comm.jar should be placed in:<br />
<br />
%JAVA_HOME%/lib<br />
<br />
%JAVA_HOME%/jre/lib/ext<br />
<br />
win32com.dll should be placed in:<br />
<br />
%JAVA_HOME%/bin<br />
<br />
%JAVA_HOME%/jre/bin<br />
<br />
%windir%System32<br />
<br />
javax.comm.properties should be placed in:<br />
<br />
%JAVA_HOME%/lib<br />
<br />
%JAVA_HOME%/jre/lib<br />
<br />
Step 2: Run this program to check Port Detection.<br />
import java.io.*;<br />
import java.util.Enumeration;<br />
import javax.comm.*;<br />
public class ListPorts<br />
{<br />
public static void main(String args[]) throws ClassNotFoundException, InstantiationException, IllegalAccessException<br />
{<br />
    CommDriver commDriver = null; <br />
    String driverName = &quot;com.sun.comm.Win32Driver&quot;; // or get as a JNLP property<br />
    commDriver = (CommDriver) Class.forName(driverName).newInstance();<br />
    commDriver.initialize();<br />
Enumeration ports = CommPortIdentifier.getPortIdentifiers();<br />
while (ports.hasMoreElements()) {<br />
CommPortIdentifier port = (CommPortIdentifier)ports.nextElement();<br />
String type;<br />
switch (port.getPortType()) {<br />
case CommPortIdentifier.PORT_PARALLEL:<br />
type = &quot;Parallel&quot;; <br />
break;<br />
case CommPortIdentifier.PORT_SERIAL:<br />
type = &quot;Serial&quot;; <br />
break;<br />
default: /// Shouldn't happen<br />
type = &quot;Unknown&quot;; <br />
break;<br />
}<br />
System.out.println(port.getName() + &quot;: &quot; + type);<br />
}<br />
}<br />
}<br />
<br />
